The goal is the same transparency your team would get from an in-person meeting.\n</p>\n</div>\n<div class=\"col-md-6\">\n<p class=\"question\">\nWhat if my team spans multiple time zones?\n</p>\n<p class=\"answer\">\nStatus Hero has been designed and tested to handle this elegantly. Time zones and notification times can be adjusted for each individual team member.\n</p>\n</div>\n<div class=\"col-md-6\">\n<p class=\"question\">\nDo team members need to download an app?\n</p>\n<p class=\"answer\">\nNope. Status Hero uses existing communication channels (email, SMS, <a href=\"/slack\">Slack</a>, <a href=\"/spark\">Cisco Spark</a>, and <a href=\"/hipchat\">HipChat</a>).\n</p>\n</div>\n<div class=\"col-md-6\">\n<p class=\"question\">\nDo team members need to setup an account too?\n</p>\n<p class=\"answer\">\nNegative. Secure, single-use magic links are used in all notifications, so checking in is as easy as clicking on a link in an email or SMS.\n</p>\n</div>\n<div class=\"col-md-6\">\n<p class=\"question\">\nCan I adjust notification settings by team member?\n</p>\n<p class=\"answer\">\nYes, and you can skip sick days and holidays. In fact, team members can do this for themselves.\n</p>\n</div>\n<div class=\"col-md-6\">\n<p class=\"question\">\nWhat about our JIRA/Trello/TFS/Github management tools?\n</p>\n<p class=\"answer\">\nStatus Hero sits atop more detailed ticket and task management systems by focusing on the gist of the work: 1-2 brief daily goals per person.\n</p>\n</div>\n<div class=\"col-md-6\">\n<p class=\"question\">\nCan I create and/or belong to multiple teams?\n</p>\n<p class=\"answer\">\nYes. With a single login email address you can create new teams, belong to other teams, and switch between teams within Status Hero.\n</p>\n</div>\n<div class=\"col-md-6\">\n<p class=\"question\">\nDoes Status Hero work with smartphones?\n</p>\n<p class=\"answer\">\nYes. Check-in forms and reports can be used with any device - desktop, mobile, or tablet.\n</p>\n</div>\n<div class=\"col-md-6\">\n<p class=\"question\">\nWhat about security?\n</p>\n<p class=\"answer\">\nWe've gone to great lengths to keep your data secure and confidential, with enterprise-grade precautions. <a href=\"/security\">Read more about security</a>.\n</p>\n</div>\n<div class=\"col-md-6\">\n<p class=\"question\">\nDo I need to involve my IT department?\n</p>\n<p class=\"answer\">\nNo. Status Hero works independently of corporate servers.\n</p>\n</div>\n<div class=\"col-md-6\">\n<p class=\"question\">\nI have more questions!\n</p>\n<p class=\"answer\">\nWe're happy to help. <a href=\"/contact\">Drop us a line.</a>\n</p>\n</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n</section>\n\n<section class=\"anchor benefits\" id=\"benefits\">\n<div class=\"container\">\n<h2>\nWhy Status Hero?\n</h2>\n<div class=\"row\">\n<div class=\"col-md-7 col-md-offset-1 col-sm-8 col-sm-offset-0 col-xs-12\">\n<h3>\nConnect Remote, Virtual, or Distributed Teams\n</h3>\n<p>\nStatus Hero collects and documents off-hour status updates that would otherwise get lost in emails, work tickets, or chat logs.\n</p>\n</div>\n<div class=\"col-md-2 col-sm-3 hidden-xs\">\n<div class=\"benefit-graphic\">\n<img src=\"/assets/stick-connect-bc556b3cc1c9a17d3ad1625fe8513e79e33ebceee4f186a2ef6f4c2dd7aa1d10.png\" alt=\"Stick connect\">\n</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"row\">\n<div class=\"col-md-2 col-md-offset-1 col-sm-3 col-sm-offset-0 hidden-xs\">\n<div class=\"benefit-graphic\">\n<img src=\"/assets/stick-noise-1ff6bf0beefb161457b1ccf5daf9102bdc84d11aae7975f60178b9fb5d115f34.png\" alt=\"Stick noise\">\n</div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"col-md-7 col-sm-8\">\n<h3>\nCut Through the Project Management Noise\n</h3>\n<p>\nFind out with a sentence or two from each team member whether everyone is working effectively towards specific goals.\n</p>\n</div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"row\">\n<div class=\"col-md-7 col-md-offset-1 col-sm-8 col-sm-offset-0 col-xs-12\">\n<h3>\nEliminate Status &amp; Stand-up Meetings\n</h3>\n<p>\n\"Can you hear me?\" \"Nope!\"\" Something always seems to go wrong with all-hands multi-point meetings. Status Hero delivers all of the value of a status meeting without the wasted time, scheduling, or tech hassle.&nbsp;\n</p>\n</div>\n<div class=\"col-md-2 col-sm-3 hidden-xs\">\n<div class=\"benefit-graphic\">\n<img src=\"/assets/stick-happy-3e1b9e7860d5b73af3a66ed6c3c12c6dbfb74c0b691d208345b700135bec83ba.png\" alt=\"Stick happy\">\n</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"row\">\n<div class=\"col-md-2 col-md-offset-1 col-sm-3 col-sm-offset-0 hidden-xs\">\n<div class=\"benefit-graphic\">\n<img src=\"/assets/stick-transparency-64e79874cf0374cc7dc5c429872fa0eb58ab6ee1df4e0e17097d26b492edc7f2.png\" alt=\"Stick transparency\">\n</div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"col-md-7 col-sm-8\">\n<h3>\nPromote Transparency &amp; Trust\n</h3>\n<p>\nTrust is built when everyone understands how each team member contributes. More trust means quicker decisions, smoother collaboration, and ultimately a&nbsp;happier and more productive team.\n</p>\n</div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"row\">\n<div class=\"col-md-7 col-md-offset-1 col-sm-8 col-sm-offset-0 col-xs-12\">\n<h3>\nBetter Software Estimates\n</h3>\n<p>\nWhen team members get into the rhythm of setting daily goals, they'll get better at setting expectations for their work.
